	<script type="text/javascript">

		$(function() {
			setTimeout(function() { window.focus(); }, 10000);
		});

		$(document).on('keypress', function () {

			// undgå problemer med fokus i ie.
			if (window.parent != null && window.parent !== window)
				return;

			var tb = $('#schoolsdiv :input:first');
			if (!tb.length) {
				tb = $('<input></input>');
				tb.on('keydown', function (e) {
					if (e.keyCode == 27) {
						tb.remove();
						filterList(null);
					}
				});
				var filterList = function(q) {
					var matcher = q ? AutocompleteUtility.CreateMatcher(q) : (function (t) { return true; });

					$('#schoolsdiv > div').each(function () {
						if ($(this).find(':input').length)
							return;
						var t = $(this).text();
						var ok = matcher(t) || /vis alle skoler/i.test(t);
						$(this).css('display', ok ? '' : 'none');
					});
				};
				tb.on('input', function(e) {
					var q = $(e.target).val();
					filterList(q);
				});
				$('<div></div>').append(tb).insertBefore($('#schoolsdiv > div:first'));
			}
			tb.focus();
		})

	</script>

</div>
	<script type="text/javascript">

		$(function() {
			setTimeout(function() { window.focus(); }, 10000);
		});

		$(document).on('keypress', function () {

			// undgå problemer med fokus i ie.
			if (window.parent != null && window.parent !== window)
				return;

			var tb = $('#schoolsdiv :input:first');
			if (!tb.length) {
				tb = $('<input></input>');
				tb.on('keydown', function (e) {
					if (e.keyCode == 27) {
						tb.remove();
						filterList(null);
					}
				});
				var filterList = function(q) {
					var matcher = q ? AutocompleteUtility.CreateMatcher(q) : (function (t) { return true; });

					$('#schoolsdiv > div').each(function () {
						if ($(this).find(':input').length)
							return;
						var t = $(this).text();
						var ok = matcher(t) || /vis alle skoler/i.test(t);
						$(this).css('display', ok ? '' : 'none');
					});
				};
				tb.on('input', function(e) {
					var q = $(e.target).val();
					filterList(q);
				});
				$('<div></div>').append(tb).insertBefore($('#schoolsdiv > div:first'));
			}
			tb.focus();
		})

	</script>

		$(function() {
			setTimeout(function() { window.focus(); }, 10000);

		$(document).on('keypress', function () {

			// undgå problemer med fokus i ie.
			if (window.parent != null && window.parent !== window)
				return;

			var tb = $('#schoolsdiv :input:first');
			if (!tb.length) {
				tb = $('<input></input>');
				tb.on('keydown', function (e) {
					if (e.keyCode == 27) {
						tb.remove();
						filterList(null);
					}
				});
				var filterList = function(q) {
					var matcher = q ? AutocompleteUtility.CreateMatcher(q) : (function (t) { return true; });

					$('#schoolsdiv > div').each(function () {
						if ($(this).find(':input').length)
							return;
						var t = $(this).text();
						var ok = matcher(t) || /vis alle skoler/i.test(t);
						$(this).css('display', ok ? '' : 'none');
					});
				};
				tb.on('input', function(e) {
					var q = $(e.target).val();
					filterList(q);
				});
				$('<div></div>').append(tb).insertBefore($('#schoolsdiv > div:first'));
			}
			tb.focus();
		})

	</script>

		$(document).on('keypress', function () {

			// undgå problemer med fokus i ie.
			if (window.parent != null && window.parent !== window)
				return;

			var tb = $('#schoolsdiv :input:first');
			if (!tb.length) {
				tb = $('<input></input>');
				tb.on('keydown', function (e) {
					if (e.keyCode == 27) {
						tb.remove();
						filterList(null);
					}
				});
				var filterList = function(q) {
					var matcher = q ? Autocomplete.CreateMatcher(q) : (function (t) { return true; });

					$('#schoolsdiv > div').each(function () {
						if ($(this).find(':input').length)
							return;
						var t = $(this).text();
						var ok = matcher(t) || /vis alle skoler/i.test(t);
						$(this).css('display', ok ? '' : 'none');
					});
				};
				tb.on('input', function(e) {
					var q = $(e.target).val();
					filterList(q);
				});
				$('<div></div>').append(tb).insertBefore($('#schoolsdiv > div:first'));
			}
			tb.focus();
		})

	</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">

		$(function() {
			setTimeout(function() { window.focus(); }, 10000);
		});

		$(document).on('keypress', function () {

			// undgå problemer med fokus i ie.
			if (window.parent != null && window.parent !== window)
				return;

			var tb = $('#schoolsdiv :input:first');
			if (!tb.length) {
				tb = $('<input></input>');
				tb.on('keydown', function (e) {
					if (e.keyCode == 27) {
						tb.remove();
						filterList(null);
					}
				});
				var filterList = function(q) {
					var matcher = q ? Autocomplete.CreateMatcher(q) : (function (t) { return true; });

					$('#schoolsdiv > div').each(function () {
						if ($(this).find(':input').length)
							return;
						var t = $(this).text();
						var ok = matcher(t) || /vis alle skoler/i.test(t);
						$(this).css('display', ok ? '' : 'none');
					});
				};
				tb.on('input', function(e) {
					var q = $(e.target).val();
					filterList(q);
				});
				$('<div></div>').append(tb).insertBefore($('#schoolsdiv > div:first'));
			}
			tb.focus();
		})

	</script>

		$(function() {
			setTimeout(function() { window.focus(); }, 10000);
		});

		$(document).on('keypress', function () {

			// undgå problemer med fokus i ie.
			if (window.parent != null && window.parent !== window)
				return;

			var tb = $('#schoolsdiv :input:first');
			if (!tb.length) {
				tb = $('<input></input>');
				tb.on('keydown', function (e) {
					if (e.keyCode == 27) {
						tb.remove();
						filterList(null);
					}
				});
				var filterList = function(q) {
					var matcher = q ? Autocomplete.CreateMatcher(q) : (function (t) { return true; });

					$('#schoolsdiv > div').each(function () {
						if ($(this).find(':input').length)
							return;
						var t = $(this).text();
						var ok = matcher(t) || /vis alle skoler/i.test(t);
						$(this).css('display', ok ? '' : 'none');
					});
				};
				tb.on('input', function(e) {
					var q = $(e.target).val();
					filterList(q);
				});
				$('<div></div>').append(tb).insertBefore($('#schoolsdiv > div:first'));
			}
			tb.focus();
		})

	</script>
